PolicyAuditLogger with the specified configuration.\n// If output is nil, logs will be sent to the default logger.\n// If useJSON is true, logs will be formatted as JSON.\nfunc {\n\tpal.Lock()\n\tdefer pal.Unlock()\n\n\t// Build the structured log fields\n\tfields := logrus.Fields{\n\t\tlogfields.Identity: identity,\n\t\t\"policy\":           policy,\n\t\t\"verdict\":          verdict,\n\t\t\"reason\":           reason,\n\t}\n\n\tscopedLog := pal.logger.WithFields(fields)\n\n\t// Log based on verdict type\n\tswitch verdict {\n\tcase decision: DENY\")\n\tcase VerdictUndecided:\n\t\tscopedLog.WithField(\"auditLevel\", \"decision\").Debug(\"Policy decision: UNDECIDED\")\n\t}\n\n\t// If JSON output is configured, also write structured JSON output\n\tif pal.useJSON && pal.output != nil {\n\t\tpal.writeJSONAuditLog(fields)\n\t}\n}\n\n// LogEvaluation logs a complete policy evaluation with context, selector cache, and *SelectorCache,\n\tresult interface{},\n) {\n\tpal.Lock()\n\tdefer pal.Unlock()\n\n\t// Build the structured log fields\n\tfields := logrus.Fields{\n\t\t\"policyKey\": policyKey,\n\t\t\"result\":    result,\n\t}\n\n\t// Add context information if available\n\tif ctx != nil {\n\t\tif deadline, ok := ctx.Deadline(); ok {\n\t\t\tfields[\"deadline\"] = deadline\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\t// Add selector cache logrus.Level) {\n\tpal.Lock()\n\tdefer pal.Unlock()\n\tpal.logLevel = level\n}\n\n// GetLogLevel returns the current log level of the audit logger.\nfunc (pal *PolicyAuditLogger) GetLogLevel()
